<p>The <b>1995 Caribbean Cup</b> (known as the <b><a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_Shell" title="Royal Dutch Shell">Shell</a> Caribbean Cup</b> for sponsorship reasons) was the seventh edition of the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Cup" title="Caribbean Cup">Caribbean Cup</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> championship of the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a>, one of the <a href="/wiki/CONCACAF" title="CONCACAF">CONCACAF</a> zones. The final stage was hosted by <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">Jamaica</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Islands" title="Cayman Islands">Cayman Islands</a>.</p>
<p></p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="First_Round_4">First Round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1995_Caribbean_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: First Round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Group_A">Group A</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1995_Caribbean_Cup&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Group A">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table class="wikitable" style="text-align: center;">
<tr>
<th width="230">Team</th>
<th width="20"><abbr title="Points">Pts</abbr></th>
<th width="20"><abbr title="Played">Pld</abbr></th>
